######################
# JAP New OOB Events #
#################################################################################################################################
# This is basically un upgrade/update of Maneman's JAP OOB Events (file is zBI_JAP_EventOOBs.txt)								#
# Rework is based upon wikipedia, niehorster 1941 OOB and Leland Ness book: Rikugun: Guide to Japanese Ground Forces 1937-1945	#
# Design to fit with new 1936 starting OOB and games mechanisms on units production.											#
#################################################################################################################################s


#####################################################################################
# ALLOW historical JAP OOB Events (HQ, divisions, brigades creations or upgrades)	#
#####################################################################################
country_event = {

	id = 33501
		
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1936.1.5
		not = { has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes }
		not = { has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_no }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33501"
	desc = "EVTDESC33501"
	picture = "JAPevent33501"

	
	option = {
		name = "Allow the events" # ok
		set_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "unique_JAP_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		supplies = -5000
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"  # no
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "no_JAP_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		set_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
#####################################################################################
# ALLOW formation of HQ, Divisions and Brigades for JAP Southern Seas Campaign		#
#####################################################################################
country_event = {

	id = 33502
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1941.6.1
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		not = { has_country_flag = JAP_Southern_Seas_Expansion }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33502"
	desc = "EVTDESC33502"
	picture = "JAPevent33502"

	
	option = {
		name = "Prepare troops for a southern campaign..." # ok
		set_country_flag = JAP_Southern_Seas_Expansion
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "JAP_Southern_Seas_Expansion_Preparation"
			duration = 210
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"  # no
		set_country_flag = JAP_Southern_Seas_Expansion
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
#########################################################################################
# ALLOW historical JAP Desperate measures Events (HQ, division) JAP is loosing war   	#
#########################################################################################
#USA is theatening Japan mainland
country_event = {

	id = 33503
		
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		war_with = USA
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		not = { has_country_flag = JAP_desperate_measures_OOB }
		
		10642 = { controller = { faction = allies } } #Allies control Iwo Jima
		
		5759 = { controller = { faction = allies } } #Allies control Okinawa
		
		5966 = { controller = { faction = allies } } #Allies control Saipan
		
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33503"
	desc = "EVTDESC33503"
	picture = "JAPevent33503"

	
	option = {
		name = "We need these troops to protect Japan!"
		set_country_flag = JAP_desperate_measures_OOB
		USA = { country_event = 33505 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
#SOV is theatening Japan mainland
country_event = {

	id = 33504
		
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		war_with = SOV
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		not = { has_country_flag = JAP_desperate_measures_OOB }
		
		4522 = { controller = { faction = comintern } } #Soviet Union controls Chongjin
		
		7009 = { controller = { faction = comintern } } #Soviet Union controls Toyohara - South Sakhalin Island
		
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33504"
	desc = "EVTDESC33504"
	picture = "JAPevent33503"

	
	option = {
		name = "We need these troops to protect Japan!"
		set_country_flag = JAP_desperate_measures_OOB
		SOV = { country_event = 33506 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

###################################
# Shanghai battle linked events   #

#Recall 24th Independant Mixed Brigade from Shanghai
country_event = {
	id = 33507

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1936.4.10
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33507"
	desc = "EVTDESC33507"
	picture = "JAPevent33507"
	
	option = {
		name = "This brigade will be usefull in Manchuria."
		set_country_flag = recall_24th_IMB
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		load_oob = JAP/JAP_24th_IMB.txt
    } 

	option = {
		name = "No, this force is needed in Shanghai."
		set_country_flag = 24th_IMB_stays_in_Shanghai
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Battle of Shanghai starts - Shanghai is ceded to JAP
country_event = {

	id = 33508
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		date = 1937.8.9
        or = {
            5519 = { controlled_by = JAP }
            5573 = { controlled_by = JAP }
            5599 = { controlled_by = JAP }
        }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33508"
	desc = "EVTDESC33508"
	picture = "JAPevent33508"

	option = {
		name = "So be it..."			
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		5542 = { add_core = JAP secede_province = JAP remove_core = CHI}		# Shanghai is seceded to Japan		
		JAP = { country_event = 33509 }
	}
}

# Battle of Shanghai starts - Japanese garrison is formed in Shanghai
country_event = {

	id = 33509
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33509"
	desc = "EVTDESC33509"
	picture = "JAPevent33508"

	option = {
		name = "So be it..."	
		add_core = 5542
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		load_oob = JAP/JAP_Shanghai_1.txt
	}
}

#Battle of Shanghai - 24th Independant Mixed Brigade have stayed in Shanghai
country_event = {
	id = 33510

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1937.8.12
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		has_country_flag = 24th_IMB_stays_in_Shanghai
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33510"
	desc = "EVTDESC33510"
	picture = "JAPevent33510"
	
	option = {
		name = "Fill the gaps with everything we have!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		load_oob = JAP/JAP_Shanghai_2.txt
	}
}

		supplies = 1500
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33511"

		name = "Rush reinforcements to Shanghai!"

		remove_brigade = "Dai-11 Kihei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Dai-11 Kohei rentai"

#Send more troops to Shanghai
country_event = {
	id = 33512

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1937.9.11
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_1937_Div_raised
		manpower = 4
		supplies = 2000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33512"
	desc = "EVTDESC33512"
	picture = "JAPevent33512"

		name = "Send more troops to Shanghai!"

		remove_brigade = "Dai-9 Sampohei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Dai-9 Kihei rentai"

# Formation of IJA Armygroups  #
################################
#Form China Expeditionary Army
country_event = {
	id = 33513

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1939.9.12
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		manpower = 3
		supplies = 1000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33513"
	desc = "EVTDESC33513"
	picture = "JAPevent33513"
	
	option = {
		name = "Let's form this HQ!"
		manpower = -3
		supplies = -1000
		officer_pool = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = JAP has_country_flag = BlackICE
                    total_ic = 10
                    not = { total_ic = 200 }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "5IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_IV"
                    duration = 70
                }	
                load_oob = JAP/JAP_China_Exp_Army.txt
            }
        }

	id = 33599

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1940.7.10
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		manpower = 9
		supplies = 1000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33599"
	desc = "EVTDESC33599"
	picture = "JAPevent33599"
	
	option = {
		name = "Let's form this division!"
		manpower = -9
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = JAP has_country_flag = BlackICE
                    total_ic = 10
                    not = { total_ic = 200 }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_V"
                    duration = 110
                }	
                load_oob = JAP/JAP_28th_Div.txt
            }
        }
        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = JAP has_country_flag = BlackICE

#Activation of 48th Division
country_event = {
	id = 33602

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1940.11.30
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		manpower = 5
		supplies = 500
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33602"
	desc = "EVTDESC33602"
	picture = "JAPevent33602"
	
	option = {
		name = "Form this division!"
		manpower = -5
		supplies = -500
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		# removing Taiwan Mixed Brigade
		remove_brigade = "'Formosa' Shidan shireibu"
		remove_brigade = "1/2 'Formosa' Konoe rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Dai-48 Yahohei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "'Formosa' Konsei ryodan"
		remove_brigade = "'Formosa' Shichoheitai"

        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = JAP has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150
					not = { total_ic = 200 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_II"
					duration = 55
				}	
				load_oob = JAP/JAP_48th_Div.txt
			}

#Japan starts to reinforce Kwantung Army after Barbarossa
country_event = {
	id = 33652

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = { war_with = SOV }
		not = { has_country_flag = Manchukuo_Reinforcements }
		date = 1941.6.25
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33652"
	desc = "EVTDESC33652"
	picture = "JAPevent33538"
	
	option = {
		name = "Start to reinforce Kwantung Army..."
		set_country_flag = Manchukuo_Reinforcements
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		}
	option = {
		name = "No need."
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

#Yamamoto's inspection - JAP choice
country_event = {
	id = 33655

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1943.4.7
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33655"
	desc = "EVTDESC33655"
	picture = "JAPevent33655"
	
	option = {
		name = "Let's do it!"
		set_global_flag = Yamamoto_inspection
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "Yamamoto_inspection"
			duration = 90
		}
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 85 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No, it's to dangerous..."
		ai_chance = { factor = 15 }
	}
}

#Yamamoto has been shot!
country_event = {
	id = 33658
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_global_flag = Yamamoto_flight
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "EVTNAME33658"
	desc = "EVTDESC33658"
	picture = "JAPevent33658"
	
	option = {
		name = "It this a disaster!"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "Yamamoto_death"
			duration = 90
		}
		dissent = 20
		kill_leader = 102675
		kill_leader = 102290
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

		officer_pool = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Jidoshoka Shidan shireibu"
		remove_brigade = "1/2 Konoe Jidoshoka rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Konsei ryodan"
		remove_brigade = "6 Yahohei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Kihei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Shichoheitai"
	}
	option = {
		name = "No, I have other plans."
		supplies = 2000
		officer_pool = 1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

	}

	picture = "JAPevent33664"
	
	option = {
		name = "Form these divisions!"
		load_oob = JAP/JAP_1st_2nd_Guard_Div.txt
		officer_pool = -500
		manpower = -5
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		#removing 1st Guard Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Konsei Ryodan shireibu"
		remove_brigade = "1/2 Konoe rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Konsei Ryodan"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Kihei rentai"
		remove_brigade = "Konoe Konsei Ryodan Shichoheitai"
		
		#removing 2nd Guard Brigade/Division, changed so its no longer renamed for nothing, this way the player doesnt lose XP for nothing
		#remove_brigade = "Konoe Shidan shireibu"
		#remove_brigade = "3/4/5 Konoe rentai"
		#remove_brigade = "Konoe Shidan"
		#remove_brigade = "2 Konoe Yahohei rentai"
		#remove_brigade = "2 Konoe Jidosha Kohei rentai"
		#remove_brigade = "Konoe Shidan sosakutai"
		#remove_brigade = "Konoe Jidosha Shidan Shichoheitai"

	}
	option = {
		name = "No need..."
		officer_pool = 1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
#Imperial Guard Expansion (1944) - Formation of 3rd Guard Infantry Division
country_event = {
	id = 33665

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date = 1944.1.15
		has_country_flag = JAP_historical_OOB_yes
		manpower = 9
		supplies = 1000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33665"
	desc = "EVTDESC33665"
	picture = "JAPevent33664"
	
	option = {
		name = "Let's form this elite division!"
		officer_pool = -500
		manpower = -9
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = JAP has_country_flag = BlackICE
                    total_ic = 10
                    not = { total_ic = 200 }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_IV"
                    duration = 150
                }	
                load_oob = JAP/JAP_3rd_Guard_Div.txt

country_event = {

		name = "Form this Air HQ!"
		officer_pool = -500
		manpower = -5
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
